parsing and manipulation.\\n\\n- **context_impl.cc/h**: Router context implementation for request-specific routing state.\\n\\n- **vhds.cc/h**: Virtual Host Discovery Service implementation for request handling after route selection.\\n\\n- **retry_state_impl.cc/h and router_ratelimit.cc/h**: Retry and rate limiting policy implementation for routes.\\n\\n- **delegating_route_impl.cc/h**: Route delegation and wrapping implementation.\\n\\n- **debug_config.cc/h**: Debug configuration for routing decisions.\\n\\n- **route_config_update_receiver_impl.cc/h and route_provider_manager.cc/h**: Route configuration update handling.\\n\\n- **static_route_provider_impl.cc/h**: Static route provider for non-dynamic routes.\\n\\n- **shadow_writer_impl.cc/h**: Shadow traffic routing implementation.\\n\\n- **string_accessor_impl.h**: String accessor utilities for route matching.\\n\\n- **header_parser_utils.cc**: Utility functions for header parsing in routing
